STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚当失败的原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不站在神所安排的地位上；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">没有遵守神的命令。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">3.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神寻找人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">8</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">9)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">4.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">人遮蔽和推诿罪</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">8</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">12</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">13)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的审判</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">14-19)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的救赎：以皮子</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">必须有牺牲为他们流血、&#33294;命</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">作衣，遮盖他们。
  </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章
   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">33.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">蛇&rdquo;何解？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">蛇在伊甸园中比田野一切的活物更狡猾，可能也是最美丽的活物。现今的蛇已成了咒诅</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">4)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。撒但称为&ldquo;古蛇&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">12</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">9</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">14-15</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">20</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，&#29280;扮作&ldquo;光明的天使&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林后</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">11</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">14)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，向人说话，迷惑众人。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚当、夏娃犯何种罪？夏娃被蛇诱惑的教训是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚当、夏娃违背了神的禁令</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16-17)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，违背神命令的就是罪</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约壹</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。夏娃被蛇诱惑的教训主要是：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">夏娃没有牢记神的话，反而擅自说了&ldquo;也不可摸&rdquo;这句神没有说的话。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">夏娃削弱了神话语的严肃性。她说，&ldquo;免得你们死&rdquo;，不相信神所说，&ldquo;必定死&rdquo;。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">夏娃明知过犯，她明知蛇的话是违背神的谎言</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">33)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，还继续与&#29280;说话，这种行为是堕落的前奏。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">夏娃自己出头，没让亚当当头；同样，教会不能出头，要让基督在万事上占首位。
   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">夏娃受了蛇的诱惑后的行动是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">夏娃见那棵树的果子好作食物，也悦人的眼目，且是可喜爱的，能使人有智慧，就摘下果子来吃了；又给她丈夫，她丈夫也吃了。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">35.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚当、夏娃吃</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">禁</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">果后发生什么事？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们知道自己是赤身露体，便拿无花果树的叶子，为自己编作裙子。他们听见神的声音，就藏在园里的树木中躲避耶和华神的面。罪种栽入一个人里面，世世代代遗传下去。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罪带来死，死带来审判，审判带来永火。人堕落的原因，接受三个试探，是撒但一贯的伎俩：</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">眼目的情欲：看果子悦人眼目。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">肉体的情欲：好作食物吃。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">3.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">今生的骄傲：如神知道善恶。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒但</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">4000</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年以后，又试探耶稣，耶稣胜过了它，用神的话抵挡它。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">路</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">肉体的情欲：石头变饼──物质世界　</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">眼目的情欲：万国的荣华──政治世界
</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">今生的骄傲：跳下殿顶──宗教世界　</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">人堕落的结果：</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">与神隔绝，赶出神的面。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">成为撒但的俘虏。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">3.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">女人生产之苦。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">丈夫管辖女人
</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">男人汗流满面才得糊口，出汗是人的努力，不能摸圣工</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">结</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">6.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">地受咒诅，属地的不能服事属天的。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7.
</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">封闭生命之路。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">36&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">你在哪里？&rdquo;何意？亚当、夏娃的态度如何？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神呼召堕落的人能及早明白自己的本相，尽快悔改，回到神的面前。他们并没有向神承认自己的错误，亚当狡辩责任在于神赐给他的妻子夏娃，从而背叛了因神恩典而得的妻子。夏娃也同样不承认自己的错误，而把责任推卸给蛇，等于埋怨神在环境中的安排。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">37.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神给蛇的咒诅、给亚当、夏娃的刑罚是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神给蛇的咒诅是：必用肚子行走，终身吃土。&ldquo;蛇&rdquo;代表撒但</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。耶稣基督的十字架击碎了撒但的头</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">致命伤</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，摧毁撒但对人的权势</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。撒但沦落为很容易受伤的地步，因为头离地甚近</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。夏娃受的刑罚：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">怀孕和分娩的痛苦；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">恋慕丈夫，被丈夫管辖。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">必定要死。亚当受的刑罚：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">终身劳苦，才得糊口。地也因他的缘故受到咒诅。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">必定要死。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">38&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">女人的后裔要伤你的头，你要伤他的脚跟&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">人与蛇</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒但</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">之间的敌对，是象征神与那恶者之间极大的争战。这争战在人的心中及人类历史中都表现出来。女人的后裔至终要伤</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">压碎</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">蛇的头。这应许在基督完全胜过撒但时得到成全</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">--</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">这是全体信徒都能共享的一种胜利。救主基督要离弃宝座，由童女马利亚藉圣灵怀孕，给&#31042;肉身的外衣。藉着死，打伤魔鬼的头</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，魔鬼要伤害&#31042;的脚跟</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">教会</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，历代以来魔鬼不断逼迫教会，产生无数的殉道者，阴间的门不能胜过教会的根基磐石</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">-</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">基督</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，基督就是灵磐石</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">39.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神用什么预表向亚当、夏娃显出&#31042;的救恩？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神宰了祭牲，基督牺牲使全人类算为无罪</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">称义</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，基督是我们的义神使无罪的基督，不知罪的基督代替我们成为罪，叫我们在&#31042;里面成为神的义</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">算无罪</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，这是客观的地位，在主观上，尚需天天经历这个事实。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神用皮子做衣服给他们穿。显明若要恢复与神的关系，必须有流血的代价，包含着主耶稣十字架舍命流血的思想。人类必须借着主耶稣的宝血与神和好，才能蒙救赎，这个和好是借着旧约时代献上无数祭牲的赎罪祭所预表的主耶稣之死而成就的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">40.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罪带来的后果是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罪带给人类死亡，并被逐出伊甸园，即与神隔绝。真正的生命在于与神之间的交通，死亡则表示这种交通的断绝。人类要在受了咒诅、满有荆棘和蒺藜的硬土上操劳，直到死亡。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">41.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">基路伯何意？其职责是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">基路伯：神受造天使中完美的形像，有四个脸，预表基督道成肉身的四个身份：万王之王</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">狮</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，神的奴仆</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">牛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，人的样式</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，神的儿子</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">鹰</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。名意：神手中紧紧守住的，顺服神至死。职分：把守生命树的道路，不让魔鬼破坏，不让罪人进去。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">4-6</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章
原始家庭和社会的开始</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">导读</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第一个家庭生活开始：因信仰而流血</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(4</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1-8)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第一个城市生活开始：是一个凶手所建立的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(4</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">16-17)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">42.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为什么神看中了亚伯所献的祭？而不悦纳该隐所献的祭？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从亚伯看见第一次事奉的路，藉着羔羊的血，为主而活的职业。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">耶稣基督是唯一的救主，耶稣基督钉十字架是唯一的救法。
</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">徒四</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">职业是牧羊，不为吃羊肉，乃为献祭用；基督徒的职业不是为生活，乃为奉献，由神主宰拣选何种职业，劳动所得由神分配。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">献上头生羊，生命精华脂油烧的香使神喜悦。明白父母皮衣的意义，靠祭牲羊与神交通。是属天的事奉之路：因主基督的牺牲代死，人与神和好，才有资格事奉神。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">殉道之死：&ldquo;亚伯&rdquo;，一口气之意。短暂人生有永远的价值，为主而活，为主而死，因照神的旨意事奉，死在属肉体事奉神的同胞兄弟手中，如同旧人压制新人。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，见证亚伯的信心，因有更美的祭物</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">-</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">主耶稣基督，死后仍说话。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从该隐看见属于恶者魔鬼的事奉</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约壹</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">该隐的职业是为己而活，地已受咒诅，他劳苦所得属地的产物献给属天的神，如同水火不容，遭神弃绝。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">任何以人的智慧、能力来事奉神，都遭咒诅</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚伯因着信献祭给神，因此得蒙神悦纳。他的信心基于信神的启示</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；创</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，他存着单纯的信心</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">创</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">29</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，将他羊群中头生的，和羊的脂油献上。该隐的献祭不是出于信心，他心中存着恶念，他没有领会神的启示。
            </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">42.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罪伏在门前&rdquo;何意？
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">圣经里第一次出现的&ldquo;罪&rdquo;，希伯来人借用古代巴比伦的表现手法，描写罪就象守在门口向屋内的人吼叫的野兽。后来彼得把这句话用在形容诱惑信徒的撒但身上。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">43.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">该隐得到的刑罚是什么？
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">被驱逐离开他生存的土地；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">地不会为他效力。因地&#21585;了无辜者的血，所以不会给杀人犯结出果子，意指地吞掉杀人犯。比创</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">记载的对亚当的刑罚还要严重。该隐属于恶者，是魔鬼之子，第一家庭从流血开始。如同亚当里的人，神要除灭；属血气的逼迫属灵的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">加</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">29)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">44.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">凡遇见我的必杀我&rdquo;，指的是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">可以认为在该隐的近亲之外，还有许多别的人；但也可能只是表明预期人种数目在未来会急剧增长。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">45.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">该隐被逐出后，发展出罪恶的文明表现在哪些方面？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">该隐被逐出后的几个世纪里，堕落的后裔急剧膨胀，并发展出罪恶的文明：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">通过他们的名字可以看出：拉麦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">大力士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，亚太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">装扮者</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，洗拉</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">游手好闲者</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，这些名字体现出当时的暴力和追求世俗的堕落。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">通过他们的所作所为可以看出：建造城池、打造铜铁利器、弹琴吹箫等，代表着征服、压制和享乐。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">通过他们的制度，可以看出当时盛行近亲结婚和一夫多妻制。该隐独立离开神。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">曼<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第一座以诺城：与神隔绝，凶手建立。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">畜牧业祖师雅八：依靠属地之物维生。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">弹琴吹箫祖师犹八：依靠音乐满足魂。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">铜铁业祖师土八该隐：依靠武器满足凶杀欲。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第一首血腥诗拉麦：满足内心的仇恨。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神责问：&ldquo;你作了什么？&rdquo;罪种产生罪行。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的拯救：该隐的记号，赐主的挽回祭
</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约壹</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">46.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">玛土撒拉何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从玛土撒拉看见神的忍耐与信实：</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">玛土撒拉名意：死后将有洪水，射箭的人。最长寿的人：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">969</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神看一日如千年──
的信实。千年如一日── 的忍耐。不愿一人沉沦，愿人人悔改得救</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">彼后三</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，但是人刚硬到底，迎来洪水灭亡。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">46.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉麦的堕落本性表现在哪里？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">4</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">23-24</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">看出，他讥笑神禁止复仇的命令，主张一定要亲自复仇；唱出了壮年人伤他，他就会杀壮年人；少年人损害他，他就害少年人；对伤害他的人，要进行复仇</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">倍的报复。拉麦与要求神保护的该隐相反，他与神完全的割绝，丝毫设有罪的意识，充满着仇恨和复仇，体现出当时社会的残忍和惨忍，他们无视神和生命的尊严。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">47.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从何时开始，人才求告耶和华的名？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从以诺看见神喜悦他的明证：与神同行有属天的赏赐</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。从塞特时代开始，人才谦卑地承认自己的软弱和无力，向神祷告和敬拜，以感恩之心公开进行崇拜活动</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">105</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从塞特</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">新苗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">产生敬虔的后裔：</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从以挪士看见第一次的祷告：求告耶和华的名。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">耶和华：旧约出现</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7000</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">多次，耶──今在
 和──昔在   华──永在</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">48.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">形象样式和自己相似&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚当是按照神的形象被造的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">26)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，但亚当在堕落以后，生了有堕落罪人形象的儿子，日后将和亚当一样犯罪、软弱、易受各种诱惑，且落在必死的命运中。不仅是塞特，血统上属于笫一亚当的全人类都是如此。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">49.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以诺与神同行&rdquo;和&ldquo;将他取去&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以诺与神同行&rdquo;：意味着与神不断的交通，过着效法神的虔诚生活。虽然撒但的权势和诱惑蔓延在世上，但是，以诺的敬虔生活给信的人带来与神同行的盼望，&ldquo;将他取去&rdquo;的意思，也用于以利亚升天时的意思，&ldquo;将他取去&rdquo;的&ldquo;取去&rdquo;是&ldquo;拿&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(take)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，也用于以利亚升天时</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">王下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9-10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">73</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">49</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。以诺和以利亚没有经历死亡，直接进入到了乐园
</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。从以诺看见神喜悦他的明证：与神同行有属天的赏赐</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">宇宙中第一个被提的人，预表活着见主再来的被提得胜者。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">首先被提的条件：生活事奉中天天与主同行，每天奉献自己，为主而活，凡事上寻求神的安排，放弃自己的主张、目的、计划，交出主权就是舍己，接受神的安排就是背起自己的十字架。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以诺的预言</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，神将审判众人，审判不敬虔者的罪行与顶撞的话。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">50.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚的名字何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚意指&ldquo;安慰&rdquo;和&ldquo;休息&rdquo;，表明：那时代族长们生活上的困境；体现他们渴望神真正的安慰和平安的信仰。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">6</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">导读</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从挪亚看见在基督里蒙拯救──方舟
</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">彼前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">安息在基督里必得救、必得力。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚名意&ldquo;安息&rdquo;：向己死，向神活。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">进入安息，必得着能力：赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">与主同负一轭，必得安息：与主同走十架路，像主柔和谦卑，在神手中可得享安息</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">29)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。歇了自己的工</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚时代强暴，乱伦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拿非林</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，预示主再来的日子前夕</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">路</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚时代，神的灵不与属肉体的人抗争，人寿数减至</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">120</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚时代，人开始吃荤。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚时代，天降第一次大雨，就是洪水</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">参创</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挪亚开始人分成三种肤色：闪──黄。雅弗──白。含──黑。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">洪水（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9-9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章）</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">
&nbsp;神对罪的态度&mdash;审判（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5-13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">）。审判中的怜悯&mdash;方舟（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14-22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">）。挪亚进方舟，洪水来到（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章）。挪亚出方舟（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">）。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神和挪亚立约（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20-9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">）。挪亚的失败（</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20-29</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">）。挪亚献燔祭，神因着祭牲，停止怒气。立虹和平的约：不再用洪水灭地。审判用火</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">彼后</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">51.
&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的儿子们&rdquo;和&ldquo;人的女子&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有几种不同见解和争议：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹太拉比传统解释，指贵族的子女和庶民的女儿。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">认为是天使和人类的女儿。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">敬虔的塞特后裔和不敬虔的该隐的女儿。第一种解释不符合圣经的内容。第二种解释也不合理，因为本文是神对堕落人类的审判，而不是天使的堕落史，并且天使无性别，也不娶也不嫁</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">可</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">12</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">25)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。第三种解释比较合理。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">52.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">一百二十年&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
