STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13-14</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；代下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。保罗借这段预言，阐明神主权性拣选的教义</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10-23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">指出神对义和不义、光和黑暗、信和不信&ldquo;选择性的区分&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林后</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14-18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
        </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">175.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">红豆汤&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">用赤褐色豆子做成的粥，现在中东地区驹人仍然欢喜吃。以扫的肤色本来就发红，加上这次红豆汤事件，人们讥笑的口吻叫他&ldquo;以东&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">红</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">176.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">长子的名分&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">旧约时代，以色列人第一个出生的孩子所享受的特权和责任，特别是在族长时代，长子权具有的特质：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">外在特权：接续父亲，成为一家之主，处理家中大小事务</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">代下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；可以分得二份遗产</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15-17)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">内在特权：履行家庭祭司长的职分；在立约关系上成为得到属灵祝福的继承人。当然长子也附带责任，当父亲年老或去世后，担当赡养母亲和家庭的义务。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">177.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫为何轻看长子的名分？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">自从人类的始祖亚当和夏娃选择了吃禁果</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，人类都变成愚拙，分不清事物真正的价值。圣经称以扫为僭妄的人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，指他戏弄、轻看神所赐生命的神圣机会，戏弄耶稣的希律</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">路</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，及讥笑保罗传道的亚基帕</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">都是僭妄的人。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">26</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">178.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神为什么不要以撒下埃及去？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚伯拉罕在埃及经受了惨痛的失败，雅各死在埃及。对神的百姓来说，圣经中的埃及意味着试炼、训练及诱惑</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；耶</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；结</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。所以神不要以撒下埃及去。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">179.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神坚定与以撒所起的誓，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神坚定与以撒所起的誓是神与亚伯拉罕之约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16-18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">更新。约的核心依然是土地和子孙，虽然这约在以色列历史中也曾成就，但最终还是借着基督，在属灵角度得以完全成就。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">180.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒犯了亚伯拉罕曾犯的错误是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒也犯了亚伯拉罕曾犯的错误</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10-20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。父母的错误会影响子女</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11-13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。以撒因害怕说利百加是他的妹子，他因说谎被外邦人指责这是何等的羞愧。现今的信徒要以此为借鉴反省自己的信仰。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">181.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒在寄居地耕种何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒继该隐</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、挪亚</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">之后，第三次有关族长耕种的记录。也呈现出族长生活的另一面。他们不但过着游牧生活，还艰苦地开垦荒地。在生活中他们如同渴望甘露一样&#28167;慕神的祝福。神也应许祝福他们。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">182.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚比米勒何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚比米勒意为&ldquo;我父的王&rdquo;，不是人名，是历代非利士王的称号</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。这个王不象亚伯拉罕立下友好之约的亚比米勒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22-32)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。理由：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">时间之相差近一个世纪；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">古代世界极其重视誓言，立约本人不会轻易毁约。
                  </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">183.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒重新挖井何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">由于原住民的嫉妒，水井纷争带来持续的压力，以撒一行从基拉耳地逐渐移向别处。巴勒斯坦地带，土质由沙漠构成，在这里找到水源挖井极其困难。当他父亲亚伯拉罕在世之日所挖的水井，因非利士人在亚伯拉罕死后塞住了，以撒就重新挖出来，仍照他父亲所叫的，叫那些井的名字。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">184.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神向以撒说，&ldquo;不要惧怕&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不要惧怕&rdquo;是指神安慰的话语犹如一道曙光，照在所有身处逆境、绝望、苦恼的信徒身上。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">185.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒&ldquo;筑了一座坛，求告耶和华的名&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">指正式、严肃的敬拜</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(4</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">26)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。体现以撒无论走到哪里都以神为中心的信仰。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">186.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒与亚比米勒订立同盟的原因及证据为何？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">基拉耳王亚比米勒与以撒订立同盟的原因是因神祝福日渐强盛的族长以撒深感恐惧。订立同盟的证据：称签订条约之日所挖的井为盟誓即示巴</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">33)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">187.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫娶两个外邦女子的婚姻对我们有何警戒？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫曾轻看长子的名分，现在对待婚姻也如此轻率。他与两个外邦女人的婚姻可见：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">无视神的一夫一妻制度</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">讥笑敬虔先祖的纯洁婚姻</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。因而在圣经里他永远被记为&ldquo;僭妄之人&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6-9)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">188.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各为何要夺取长子权？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在旧约时代，在家中享有首生的权利，承继他父亲为一家之首，且多得一份家产（申２１：１７）。还有居住迦南地的福气和权利，并繁衍众多，成为大国（创２８：４）。雅各知道长子权的重要性，所以要夺取长子权。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">189.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒给雅各的祝福是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以撒给雅各祝福的内容：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">地上的祝福：肥沃的土地和丰足的粮食</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(27</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">属灵的祝福：统治权和祝福权</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(27</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">29)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">190.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各连续三次撒谎何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">说自己是以扫；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">说自己打猎回来；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">说神预备好了食物。从中可以得到的教训：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从数量上，一个谎言到第二个谎言；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从质量上，前面一句单纯的谎言到更严重的谎言；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各把耶和华的名字也加了进去，这与彼得第三次否认基督，加上咒诅的起誓具有相同的性质</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">69-75)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">191.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫为何怨恨雅各？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫因他父亲给雅各祝的福，就怨恨雅各。从这一点看，以扫在以撒面前流下的泪水不是悔改的泪水，而是因丧失原本属于自己的权力的气愤的泪水。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">192.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利百加为何打发雅各往拉班那里去？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">因为利百加得知以扫要杀雅各，所以利百加打发雅各往拉班那里去。雅各长达</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年的逃亡生活即将开始。这也许是对雅各用谎言欺骗父亲的惩罚。同样，即使是信徒，虽然罪可以通过悔改而被饶恕，但罪的结果往往会留下成为一根剌，通过这根刺，能够更彻底地认识自己的罪，过着谦卑的生活。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">28</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">193.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫的错误何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫把不被父母认可、没能得到父亲祝福的原因，归结于外邦出身的妻子。所以到了晚年他又结了第三次婚，这次婚姻只不过再一次证实以扫不适合作圣约继承人的事实。他的错误：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">忽视了尽管以实玛利家庭是亚伯拉罕的血统，却是从神的祝福中分离出来、在立约之外的民族；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他原来的妻子没有死亡，又没有离婚，他却因要得祝福的野心，轻忽神定下的一夫一妻制</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">36</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
           </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">194.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各出了别是巴何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各出了别是巴的意义是：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为了逃避以扫的报复；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为了从母亲的家族中娶妻，雅各离开了温暖的家和心爱的父母。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">195.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各见到的梦是什么？何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各梦见梯子的头顶着天，有神的使者在梯子上，上去下来。这梯子连接立约之神居住的天及立约之后裔居住的地，象征立约的核心</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">--</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">基督。这是为了表明只有借着成为梯子的基督，罪恶的人类才能与神有真正属灵的交通。神的使者在梯子上，上去下来：表示耶和华愿作雅各的神。耶稣自己是天地间的桥梁</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，&#31042;是唯一&ldquo;在神和人中间&hellip;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">中保&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">提前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
     </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">196.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各见梦后许愿何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各见梦后许愿从表面上看，雅各的许愿采用的是对祝福的报答形式，但在心里，却是他从信心发出的感恩许愿。说：&ldquo;神若与我同在，在我所行的路上保佑我，又给我食物吃、衣服穿，使我平平安安地回到我父亲的家，我就必以耶和华为我的神，我所立为柱子的石头也必作神的殿，凡你所赐给我的，我必将十分之一献给你。&rdquo;日后雅各还了这个愿</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(35</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。伯特利成为记念神向他的百姓显现及同在的处所。什一奉献是谦卑的信仰告白&mdash;自己的一切都是神所赐的。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">29</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">197.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">东方人之地&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">
&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">东方人之地&rdquo;：指距&#21029;是巴</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">725</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">公里的米所波大米地区。如果雅各一天的行程是</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">48</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">公里，则需</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">天能到达。
    </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">198.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">看见田间有一口井&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在游牧地区，水井是重要路标。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">199.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉结牧放羊&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当今阿拉伯游牧民族中，还经常可以看到女孩子牧放羊的身影
     </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">200.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各与拉结亲嘴&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各在众人面前与拉结亲嘴，是把她看作小妹妹，也因漫长的旅程后见到亲人的喜悦。这戏剧性的相迂是井边相迂事件之一，还包括以利以谢与利百加相迂</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、摩西与叶忒罗七个女儿相迂</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15-16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、基督与叙加城女人相迂</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6-7)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">201.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">你实在是我的骨肉&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各坦诚详细的叙述，使拉班确信他就是自己的侄子。骨肉是有血缘的亲密关系</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；撒下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">202.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各&ldquo;看这七年如同几天&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">爱情奇妙的力量，使雅各喜乐和盼望克服漫长的雇工生活。爱的确具有惊人的力量，能使人忍耐一切痛苦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4-7)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。圣徒生活在罪恶的世界，但借着对天国火热的盼望及对基督挚热的爱，才能拥有真正的喜乐。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">203.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当主人女儿出嫁时，使女也与主人女儿一同嫁过去，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">根据努斯</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(NUZI)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">泥板所记有关结婚的规定，当主人出嫁时，使女也与主人一同嫁过去，使女所生的孩子要归主人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">204.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各&ldquo;爱拉结胜似爱利亚&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各可能受到父母影响</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。另一方面，莱特夫</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(
Light foot ) </FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">博士解释，利亚象征生活在律法中的犹太人；拉结象征生活在福音之下的基督徒。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">205.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神使利亚多子，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神使利亚多子，使雅各偏爱的拉结无子，为了：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">体现神的公义，神安抚痛苦的人，使蒙福的人不致傲慢。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">根据神深切的护理及恩典。利亚通过给儿子起的名，感谢看顾自己苦情的神，告白期望得到丈夫的情怀。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">206.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利亚生了第四个儿子，起名犹大，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利亚生了第四个儿子，起名犹大。基督就是在犹大的后裔中诞生。预示所有的赞美，都应以基督为中心。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">30</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">207.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉结的错误何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在古代社会，生养众多是女人的义务及幸福，也是给丈夫最好的礼物。拉结见自己不给雅各生子，就嫉妒她姐姐，对雅各说：&ldquo;你给我孩子，不然我就死了。&rdquo;拉结的肤浅行为与哈拿形成鲜明的对照，作为同样不能生育的女人，哈拿却跪拜在神面前，流泪祈求</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">110-11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">208.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉结和利亚利用子女竞争，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为了得到丈夫宠爱，拉结和利亚两姐妹利用子女竞争，表明破坏神一夫一妻婚姻的家庭，矛盾和纷争、嫉妒和争竞不会停止。尽管如此，神还是不看他的失败，将一切引向善的方向，在历史中努力成就与亚伯拉罕、以撒、雅各立下的约。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">209.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">风茄&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">
&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">风茄&rdquo;，又被称为&ldquo;爱情之果&rdquo;兴奋剂，当时近东妇女认为这种果实可以帮助妇女怀孕。
         </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">210.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为何记录底拿的名字？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各除了底拿以外，肯定还有其他的女儿</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(46</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，但圣经只记录了这个女儿，她因强奸事件而出名</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(34</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。通常，圣经记录的女人名字：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">特殊人物的夫人：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">特殊事件的主人公。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">211.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟名字何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟名字有两个意思：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">除去羞耻&rdquo;之意。约瑟的出生表明神除去拉结婚后七年不能生育的羞耻；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">增添我一个儿子&rdquo;之意。便雅悯的出生成就了拉结这个心愿</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(35</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">212.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各与岳父拉班签订的合同有何意义？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各与岳父拉班签订合同的意义：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以娶拉结为条件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(29</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18-19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，雅各白白服事七年；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各无力对抗故意毁约的拉班，为了拉结只好再服事七年</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(29</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第三个合同中，雅各坚决要求工价。这个合同一直到他照神吩咐</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">逃出巴旦亚兰，持续</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年之久。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">31</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">213.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">回到我本乡本土&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉结生约瑟之后，雅各的年纪已经</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">91</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁，离开故乡迦南地也有</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">个年头。从人的角度看，雅各有许多缺点，但可贵的他持有强烈的立约继承人的意识，对神的应许充满信心。他向岳父大胆宣告自己要回到本地的决定。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">214.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各的工价，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各的工价：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">除去纯白的绵羊，有斑、点、黑色的绵羊属于雅各；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">除纯黑山羊外，有斑、点的山羊归雅各所有。中东地区，十之八、九的绵羊是白色，山羊是黑色，从这点来看，这个条件对雅各极其不利。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">215.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">杨树、杏树、枫树的嫩枝，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">杨树、杏树、枫树的嫩枝：这些植物表皮呈黑色或深棕，里面纯白、油光，将树皮不规则地&#21085;下，内部的深浅颜色显出斑点形状。
  </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">216.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">羊对着枝子配合&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">饮水的羊在交配时看到这些斑点，这些花纹就秧在受胎的小羊身上。不是雅各的方法有了效果，而是神利用这非科学的方法作了工。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">217.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">你要回你祖父之地&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">你要回你祖父之地&rdquo;：
神的指示和应许是根据二十年前的伯特利之约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。可见，只要到了时候，神肯定有办法招&#22252;自己立约的百姓，无论他们在多么遥远的地方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28-29)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
       </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">218.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各信仰的告白是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">早先与雅各的祖父亚伯拉罕和父亲以撒同在的神，与他们立的恩约具有连续性。雅各认识到这一点，说出他的信仰告白。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">219.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">十次&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">并非如字面所示只有十次</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">民</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；伯</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，而指&ldquo;尽可能常常&rdquo;或&ldquo;只要有机会&rdquo;。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">220.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">跳母羊的公羊&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">指动物的交配行为。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">221.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">我是伯特利的神&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神记念这个含有特殊意义的地方。这里是亚伯拉罕进入迦南地，第一次筑坛的地方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7-8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3-4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，也是神向逃亡路上的雅各显现，并与他签下梯子之约的地方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
         </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">222.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">现今你起来&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">信仰决断的一瞬间。人生短暂，像草、雾转瞬即逝</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">90</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；传</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；雅</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；彼前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，应抓住一切机会跟从神。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">223.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当雅各要回祖父之地，他的两个妻有何反应？何故？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各的两个妻子拉结和利亚同意丈夫返回迦南地的建议，因为</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们一直对父亲把自己与雅各十四年的工价作为交换心怀不满；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">父亲拉班不再把她们当作女儿，而当作已出嫁约外人。她们也不再指望从父亲那里分得任何产业；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在雅各致富的过程中，感觉到神约祝福与护理。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">224.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神像&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">意为&ldquo;平安度日&rdquo;，作为家庭守护神，用于祈福、占术、及神谕</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">结</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；亚</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">通常是木质</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13-16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">或银质</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">类似人的偶像，有小型的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，也有像真人那么大的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。神像不见，拉班马上察觉到了，可以看出神像与日常生活关系密切。虽经多次抵制神像行动，这种俗习在巴比伦时代依然存留。
                   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">225.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">说好说歹&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">说好说歹&rdquo;字面的意思&ldquo;从善到恶&rdquo;。神警告拉班不可对雅各采取任何行动，让他平安返回故乡。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">226.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉班为何指责雅各？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉班指责雅各的原因主要是：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">没有告&#21029;而悄悄地溜走；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">偷走自己家中的神像。
               </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">227.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神像对拉班为何重要？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神像对拉班如此重要的原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从祖先传下来的家庭守护神</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">18</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">24)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">给子女合法分配财产的证物。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">228.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不容谁存活&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹太拉比以预言的形式理解族长的这句话，解释为&ldquo;他不能享满自己的寿&rdquo;。因为这事没过多久，偷神像的当事人拉结就因难产而死</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(35</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16-20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各的话成了咒诅，他当时只顾为自己的清白辩护，并未顾到其他家人，因而说话过分草率、欠周。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">229.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">驮篓&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">近东或中东地区富有的女人都使用这样的&ldquo;驮篓&rdquo;，形状象一个舒适的安乐椅，上面铺着一层厚厚的地毯，犹如一个大背篓或摇篮，很容易在下面藏一些小东西。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">230.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">身上不便&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">
