<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在摩西律法</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">之前，东方很多地区的人就认为女人的月经不洁净。印度甚至不允许经期的女人参加任何宗教仪式。拉班没有检查拉结，因为：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">剪羊毛的庆典时期，不想因女儿的不洁污秽自己；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">无法想象经期女儿敢把守护神坐在身子下面。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">231.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉班与雅各立约，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉班与雅各立约，就是米斯巴之约：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">立约的标记：在基列的山地上用石头立成柱子和石堆；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约的名称：拉班用亚兰语称为&ldquo;伊迦尔撒哈杜他&rdquo;，雅各用希伯来语称为&ldquo;迦累得&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">47)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">立约的&#20839;容：不可苦待拉班的女儿，另娶妻子；不可越过石柱侵犯对方。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">232.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">伊迦尔撒哈杜他&hellip;迦累得&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> &ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">伊迦尔撒哈杜他&hellip;迦累得&rdquo;：
含有&ldquo;以石堆为证&rdquo;之意。两种语言都属闪族语系，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">47</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">是圣经第一次出现亚兰言语，证明亚伯拉罕的故乡米所波大米使用亚兰语或迦勒底语，以撒和雅各的故乡迦南地使用希伯来语。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">233.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">米斯巴&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> &ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">米斯巴&rdquo;
为希伯来语，意为&ldquo;守卫台&rdquo;。迦累得是另一名称，意为&ldquo;愿神鉴察彼此是否遵守约定&rdquo;。日后在耶弗他和撒母耳时代，这里成了以色列重要的历史舞台</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5-16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17-24)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">234.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚伯拉罕&hellip;拿鹤&hellip;他们父亲的神&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉班的泛神论观，他分不清亚伯拉罕的神和拿鹤、他拉的神。或许可能是&ldquo;他们父亲他拉的众神&rdquo;，反映出拉班的多神信仰背景</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年前，雅各已经在伯特利见到&ldquo;以撒的神&rdquo;。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">笫</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">32</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">233.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的使者&rdquo;，何意？&ldquo;神的使者遇见他&rdquo;，目的何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的使者&rdquo;：在雅各逃亡路上，曾在伯特利向他显现</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">过的神的天使，再次出现在他归乡的旅程中，目的是：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">让他铭记神始终与他同在的事实；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">使他确信神将保护他脱离以扫复仇的手，正如在拉班的各样诡计中保护他一样。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">234.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的军兵&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的军兵&rdquo;
由天使组成，主要任务之一就是在信徒周围守护、确保安全</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">91</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。基督也提到这支神圣军队存在</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">53)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。在雅各一行返回迦南的路上出现这支军队意义：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">欢迎与神立约的主人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">归回本土；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">安慰惧怕以扫报复的雅各，这支军队将成为他的护卫队。这个地方位于迦累得和雅博河之间。
             </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">235.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">玛哈念&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">玛哈念&rdquo;是&ldquo;两队军兵&rdquo;的意思。地在基列北部，雅博渡口以北（创３２：２）。雅各曾在该地遇见神的使者。大卫逃避押沙龙时，曾来到该地（撒下１７：２７）。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">236.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">西珥地&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为一山地，位于死海东南，即以东地（创３２：３）。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大边界之山岭（书１５：１０），在基列耶琳之西。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">237.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为何称哥哥以扫为我王？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">希伯来人常表示谦卑的方式，尽量降低自己，抬高对方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">238.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有牛、驴、羊群、仆婢&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各借使者向以扫详细介绍自己的财产，目的：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">表明自己对父亲的产业绝无迷惑；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">没有打算依靠哥哥，给他添负担；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">表明回来纯粹是因对本土、对父母的思念以及希望得到哥哥为宽恕。
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">239.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">带来四百人&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫不愧为依靠刀剑生活的人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(27</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">40)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，他已成为拥有强大战斗力的部落族长。可以看出他的行动，分明是要进行报复的宣战，而不是为了和解。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">240.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各面对强势的哥哥，如何向神祷告？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">
<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">亚伯拉罕为所多玛城的祷告</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22-32)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，可以看成对话式代祷。雅各是以神的恩约为凭据</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13-15)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，单向神祈求。雅各向神祷告说；&ldquo;你曾说；&lsquo;我必定厚待你，使你的后裔如海边的沙，多得不可胜数，&rsquo;&rdquo;
  </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">241.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拿礼物&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拿礼物：不是单纯的礼物，是表示和好及请求饶恕的进贡。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">242.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅博&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">由死海东北发源，与约但河汇流，距死海约３８公里（民２１：２４）。&ldquo;雅博&rdquo;意思从&ldquo;撕打&rdquo;而来，这条河的名字有&ldquo;摔跤手&rdquo;之意，后人为记念雅各在这里的特殊经历而取名。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">243.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各与天使摔跤，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">摔跤</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(abaq)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的词根具有&ldquo;尘土飞扬地撕打&rdquo;
之意，这可能与那条河的名字&ldquo;雅博&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(32</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有关，含有&ldquo;紧紧抱住躺下&rdquo;
或&ldquo;紧紧贴住&rdquo;
之意，生动地描写雅各祷告的样子。雅各的祷告是决一胜负的祷告，如同摔跤般毫不懈怠，他恳求祝福，使用所有力量</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">路</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">44)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">祷告。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">244.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有一个人&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> &ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有一个人&rdquo;
是指耶和华的天使</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(the
angel of God ) </FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；也可认为是被称为耶和华的使者</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、道成肉身之前的基督。
            </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">245.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">大腿窝&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> <FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">字面意思是指&ldquo;臀部的窝&rdquo;
，就是大腿上窝进去部位</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">大概是坐骨处的肌肉</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各在身体上，以色列人在他们饮食条例中，留下一个永久的标记，记念他与神决定性的相迂经历。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">246.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神使雅各&#25914;名为以色列，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神使雅各&#25914;名为以色列，起名的行为代表命名者的所有权和统治权。雅各之名含有&ldquo;欺骗夺去&rdquo;之意，将其换成含有&ldquo;神的王子&rdquo;之意的&ldquo;以色列&rdquo;，表明：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">原本失败的名字受祝福后成为属灵、胜利的名字；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">根据伯特利之约，雅各正式成为立约的继承人。
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">247.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">何必问我的名&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">日后玛挪亚询问耶和华使者的名字时</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，也得到同样的答复。人类有限的智慧无法理解这个神奇惊人的名字。
         </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">248.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&#27608;努伊勒&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">意思就是&ldquo;神的面&rdquo;。在疏割以东约６公里，是宗教圣地。雅各曾在雅博渡口与神的使者摔跤（创３２：３０）。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">249.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以色列人不吃大腿窝的筋，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为了记念雅各在雅博渡口的摔跤事件，直到现在犹太人不吃动物屁股和大腿连接处的筋。他们认为大腿窝的筋和血一样</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，通过与神的接触成为圣物。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">33</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">250.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各举目观看&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各抬起眼睛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">看</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&#38755;对以扫。罪人只有悔改才能除去内心的恐惧，得到真正的平安</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约壹</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
        </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">252.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各为何排列孩子和妻子的顺序？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从雅各排列孩子和妻子的顺序中，明显看出他对不同家庭成员的偏爱心理和行为</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(29</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">30)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">253.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各一连七次俯伏在地，何意？
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">古代对王或占领者的礼仪，从远处开始七次俯伏靠近对方。雅各所采取的表示真心悔改过去的错误，恳求和解的诚意。
  </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">254.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫与雅各相见时的情况意味着什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各的谦卑征服了以扫的心，这谦卑来自对神恩典的体验。此时此刻，雅各多年来尝尽了异乡艰苦的试炼。同时也显明神的护理和欣慰的微笑，因为使两兄弟在喜悦与泪水中相逢的就是历史背后的神。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">255.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">如同见了神的&#38755;&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当雅各见到哥哥以扫脸上露出亲切和热情时，他认为犹如在神脸上看到的亲切和热情。雅各显然将看到耶和华神后得以存活时的喜悦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(32</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，与这时见到以扫得以活着的喜悦联系起来。
    </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">256.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各为何拒绝以扫的保护和引领建议？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">原因为：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各一行人的前行速度慢，无法与训练有素的以扫军队相比；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们的目的地不同：以扫是西珥地；雅各是迦南地。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们的生活目标不同：以扫靠刀剑度日</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(27</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">40)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；雅各靠畜牧度日。因此，雅各只是与以扫和好，平安地与哥哥道别。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">257.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">孩子们年幼娇嫩，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当时，长子流使</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁，小儿子约瑟仅</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁。
       </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">258.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">疏割&rdquo;何意？有何重要性？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">疏割&rdquo;
的意思是&ldquo;帐篷&rdquo;，在雅博渡口以北</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">公里处，约旦河东边的山谷地带</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4-16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各一家较长时间居住此地。主要原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年奴仆似的生活苦难，从拉班家匆忙出逃，已使地身体、精神都疲惫不堪，需要个安静的地方休息恢复体力和精神。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">259.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">示剑&rdquo;城何意？雅各为何向示剑的父亲、哈抹的子孙买了地？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">希未人族长哈抹所建之城，用儿子示剑的名给城命名。位于耶路撒冷以北</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">55</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">公里，在以巴路山和基利心山之间。日后埋葬约瑟遗骨之地</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">24</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">32</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">16)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。根据神的应许</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(28</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">13)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，雅各确信迦南地早晚会属于自己及后裔，所以他凭信心买了部分土地。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">260.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各筑坛何意？&ldquo;坛&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各在那里筑了一座坛，起名叫伊利伊罗伊以色列，意思是&ldquo;神，以色列的神&rdquo;。雅各筑坛正式承认他的祖父、父亲的神也是他的神，把新买的地分别为圣献给神。这是雅各特意为&ldquo;以色列&rdquo;的神所献，是为了记念神与自己立下的伯特利之约，并给自己起名叫&ldquo;以色列&rdquo;。
坛：古代人用土或石筑成坛。向神献祭，最早记载在创８：２０。挪亚出方舟后为耶和华筑了一座坛。早期的坛较简单不雕刻，以色列人进迦南后，坛逐渐有了定式。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">34</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">261.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各女儿底拿要见那地的女子们，何意？发生了什么事？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">底拿和约瑟的出生日期差不多</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21-24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，根据</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，底拿当时大概</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁左右。她为了观赏异地风光、要见示剑地的女子们，当时，未婚女孩在没有同伴的妇女在外很危险，结果遭受示剑的行淫、玷辱。示剑玷污底拿，也给这座城带来灭顶之灾。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">262.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">示剑家族向雅各家求婚的原因何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">示剑家族向雅各家求婚的原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">希望能够园满处理两家的婚事；通过结亲是想与以色列民结为同一民族，同享神给雅各的祝福，这是以色列人以后经常遇到的威胁，不是被异族同化，便是被消灭。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家虽然是外来客，但因与以撒和以扫有关，故具有非常大的影响力。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">263.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">人人忿恨，十分恼怒&rdquo;，何意？其问题严重性何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">人人忿恨，十分恼怒&rdquo;，是指家人极其愤怒、痛苦的状态。因为底拿被未受割礼的人玷污</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">36</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；撒下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。其问题的严重性在于：底拿不是普通人，她乃是立约之民的女儿。肉体上的犯罪，对圣约及选民以色列的名誉和自豪感带来了沉重的打击</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；撒下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">264.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">哈抹向雅各提出迎娶&#21390;拿的优惠条件是什么？
   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">
<FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">通过彼此结亲，结盟友好关系</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">答应雅各家族可以居住自己的土地，并提供经商致富的机会</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">答应要求的聘金和礼物</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11-12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。根据神的应许，雅各对迦南地有主权意识。雅各儿子们的&#24996;恨不仅仅由于家人受玷污，更是由于宗教信仰的不同，因此示剑提出的条件，对他们根本没有用。
    </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">265.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">聘金&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">聘金&rdquo;是男方家作为迎娶女子而付给女方家的财产</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。礼物是单给新娘的礼物，有时两种并用。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">266.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">凡从城门出入的男丁都受了割礼，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">凡从城门出入的男丁都受了割礼，因为</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当时&ldquo;割礼&rdquo;仪式广为人知；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">示剑对底拿爱慕之心</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在示剑城，哈抹和示剑有着极大的影响力</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19-23)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">与哈抹的想法吻合，就是联合雅各的经济和社会影响力，从而扩充自己的部落。城门口：为扩大影响力，在众人聚集的城门口宣布与以色列的关系</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，可以看出示剑对底拿的恋情非常强烈。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">267.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">西缅和利未用刀杀了城中的一切男丁，且掳掠那城，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">由于施行割礼后的炎症和发热，是行动最痛苦的时候。底拿的哥哥西缅和利未，与底拿同母的哥哥，对示剑和这城中的居民施行报复，实施血腥屠杀，分明偏离了神的旨意，是不道德、无人道的行为。因为：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们降低神圣割礼的意义，使沦为可怕报复的手段；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">报复的程度过于示剑的过失程度。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">严重背弃信义和誓言。圣经指出以恶报恶是大罪</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">39</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">44)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">268.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各深切痛苦的原因何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各深切痛苦的原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">家庭的光景与离开哈兰时的决心相反，他曾立志在迦南地兴家立业</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，但与有名望的祖父亚伯拉罕</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">和父亲以撒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">相反，因儿子的残忍报复，使这个与神立约家族的尊严，在外邦人心目中一落千丈；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">带给这个家族生存的危机</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">35</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">270.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">底拿事件后，雅各的转机是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神对于正在挫折和痛苦中的雅各说：&ldquo;起来！上伯特利去，&hellip;&rdquo;神不断重申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的话语，这给雅各才是扶持、赋予新能力的唯一盼望。神使回到&#31042;的怀抱。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">271.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">要起来，上伯特利去&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">对雅各来说，上伯特利是有特别的意义：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在他最痛苦的时候，强烈体验到神看顾他的地方；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">最纯真、真实地告白自己信仰并许愿的地方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10-20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。是雅各家恢复信仰的座右铭。当今的圣徒也一样，越觉得世上的生活痛苦、艰难，越该回到各自的伯特利，回想起初体验过的神的爱</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，让信心的膏油充满将残的信仰之火</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">弗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；腓</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">272.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">耳&#26422;上的环子，藏在示剑那里的橡树底下&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> 
<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">耳&#26422;上的环子，好象不是单纯的耳环，是以迷信为目的的耳环，上&#38755;可能刻有某种神象或咒语。藏在示剑那里的橡树底下：这里是雅各的祖父亚伯拉罕进入迦南地之后，第一次给神筑信心之坛的地方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5-7)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各把家中所有的外邦神像埋在这里；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">宣告要回到亚伯拉罕持有的纯洁信仰</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(13</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在神的约&#38755;前，所有的偶像如同死尸</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">273.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">伊勒伯特利&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">伊勒伯特利&rdquo;
指伯特利神。是雅各对神的称呼，记念神在伯特利向自己显现、赐恩。对雅各来说，那段日子是最恐惧、痛苦、艰难的时期。雅各回忆神当时赐予的恩惠，以此检验目前自己的信仰，并把将来交托给神。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">274.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利百加的奶妈底波拉死亡，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> 
<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利百加的奶妈底波拉跟随利百加从巴旦亚兰到了以撒家中</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">59)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。她常照顾利百加的后代。利百加的奶妈底波拉之死，让雅各更加思念自己的母亲。雅各和家人对她的死亡非常悲痛，向她表示真挚的敬意和哀悼，为了永远记念她，给她的墓起名。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">275.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神将雅各改名为以色列，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神曾经赐给亚伯拉罕和以撒关于土地和后裔的应许</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(17</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2-8</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">26</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2-5)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，现在神用&ldquo;以色列&rdquo;这一新名再次强调与选民所立的约。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">276.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各记念与神的相迂的行动是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各纪念与神的相迂的行动：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">立了一个石柱；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在柱子上奠酒、浇油，使其圣洁；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">给地名起名伯特利，分别为圣</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(28</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">18</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">19)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">277.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家人因拉结生便雅悯死亡的痛苦和喜悦何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉结生了约瑟，切盼第二个儿子出生</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，在她如愿以偿的时候，却在难产痛苦中死亡，使全家带来悲哀，但因第十二个儿子便雅悯的诞生带来喜悦，完整的以色列十二支派形成。
   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">278.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">拉结的墓碑何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">现在找不到墓碑的痕迹，但伯利恒至今仍有一座小坟墓，被称为拉结之墓。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">279.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">流便与父亲之妾同寝之罪带来的后果是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">流便与父亲之妾同寝，是乱伦之罪</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(49</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">4</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；林前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。他因这罪：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">永远被剥夺长子权</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">代上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">流便支派中没有出过出色的士师、预言家或君王。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">280.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各进入哈兰后与父亲相迂，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各进入哈兰后与父亲以撒保持着联系，但真正的相迂可能过了</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年。以撒年纪老迈，在即将去世前能父子相会非常重要；当以撒去世时，以扫、雅各也相迂，把以撒埋葬了。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">36</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">281.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">记载以扫的生涯及其后裔之目的何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">
<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">记载以扫的生涯及其后裔之目的：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在神政史上，这些记载与立约的百姓以色列有密切的关系。如同罗得对亚伯拉罕，以实玛利对以撒的意义。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神预言的成就</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">--&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">两国、两民族在利百加的腹中&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">23)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以立约之地迦南为中心，对照留下的人和离去者的生涯。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">282.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫的三个妻子和他们家族的记录与以前记录的有何不同？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以扫的三个妻子和他们家族的记录与以前记录的不同：</FONT></FONT></P>

<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出现差异的原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">如同&ldquo;以扫&rdquo;又被称为&ldquo;以东&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(36</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，在特殊事件中，可以有另外的名字；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">圣经中提到的父亲，有时指先祖，不一定就是父亲</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(36</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman,
