<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">没有人能园解：当时埃及有专门传达神谕和解梦的术士、博士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">8)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。两个大臣苦于在牢里，无法见到他们。解梦不是出于神吗？约瑟一直把神赐予的梦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(37</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5-9)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">记在心里，心中确信两位大臣的梦也是由神而来的超然护理。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">327.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">酒政的梦，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">根据当年记念碑和圣经的记载，当时埃及人种植葡萄并酿葡萄酒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">民</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">20</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">78</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">47)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。&ldquo;法老必提你出监&rdquo;，表示酒政被法老赦免和恢复职权</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">王下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">25</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">27</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；耶</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">52</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">31)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">328.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">膳长的梦，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">膳长的梦：三天之&#20839;，法老必斩你的头，是一种极刑，死囚的尸体不能埋葬，而是挂在树上，增加他的耻辱</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">329.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从希伯来人之地掳来的&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">希伯来人&rdquo;
字&#38755;意思是&ldquo;过来的人&rdquo;，用于描述亚伯拉罕</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(14</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的背景。在如下情况下会使用&ldquo;希伯来人&rdquo;一词：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以色列人向别的民族称呼以色列民族时</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(43</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">32</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；拿</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">别的民族称呼以色列人时</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。约瑟这样介绍自己，因他没有忘记自己是闪和雅弗支系</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(10</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、亚伯拉罕的后裔、立约的百姓</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">耶</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">330.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">我头上顶着&hellip;筐&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当时埃及男人用头顶东西，女人会扛在肩上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">331.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">斩断你的头&hellip;挂在木头上&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">斩断你的头&hellip;挂在木头上&rdquo;，这是一种极刑，死囚的尸体不能埋葬，而是挂在树上，增加他的羞辱</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">21</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">21</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">22</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">10</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">332.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不记念约瑟，竟忘了他&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不记念约瑟，竟忘了他&rdquo;，约瑟借神赐给的智慧解梦，使酒政等人的梦园解</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，但酒政却不记念约瑟，竟忘了他。此事之后，约瑟在狱中又度过了两年，接受神最后的试炼</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">333.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在神的启示历史中，梦有何重要意义？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">梦常属于神护理的范围</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">民</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；王上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；耶</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；珥</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，在神的启示历史中，梦是重要的启示手段之一。在</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，法老作的梦是决定约瑟一生重大之梦的最大一个，这是神特别计划的梦，目的是让约瑟成为埃及的宰相，在历史中成就与以色列所立的约。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">334.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老作梦的内容与约瑟解梦及对策各如何？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老作梦的内容与约瑟解梦及对策如下：</FONT></FONT></P>

			        容</FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
		<TD WIDTH=94>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">解梦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">25-28)</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
		<TD WIDTH=94>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">对策</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">29-36)</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
	</TR>
	<TR VALIGN=TOP>
		<TD WIDTH=45>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">第一个梦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1-4)</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
		<TD WIDTH=154>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">开始看见在尼罗河边有七只又美好又肥壮的母牛在芦荻中吃草；后来看见从河里上来又丑陋又干瘦的七只母牛，吃尽了那先上来的七只母牛</FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
		<TD ROWSPAN=2 WIDTH=94>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">先出来的七只肥壮的母牛及七个肥大的麦穗象征开始的七个丰年。后来的七只干瘦母牛和七个细弱麦穗象征七个严重的荒年</FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
		<TD ROWSPAN=2 WIDTH=94>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">首先任命有能力的官吏，然后设立全国范围的农业政策，在丰年期间收取</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">1/5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">的粮食储存在国库城，预备荒年</FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
	</TR>
	<TR VALIGN=TOP>
		<TD WIDTH=45>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">第二个梦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">3-7)</SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
		<TD WIDTH=154>
			<P CLASS="cjk"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 6pt">开始看见又肥大又佳美的七个麦穗；后来长了又细弱又被东风吹焦的七个麦穗吞了那先长的七个麦穗</FONT></FONT></P>
		</TD>
	</TR>
</TABLE>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">   
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">335.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">母牛&rdquo;及&ldquo;河里&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">母牛&rdquo;：在埃及，母牛是象征月神&ldquo;伊希斯&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(Isis)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的动物，与土地产量有关。为了丰收，安排又美好又肥壮的母牛出现在埃及尼罗河。&ldquo;河里&rdquo;，泛指埃及的尼罗河。这条河水多情况，决定埃及农业是否丰收。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">336.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">术士&rdquo;、&ldquo;博士&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> &ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">术士&rdquo;
：意为&ldquo;解释所隐藏神奇之事的人&rdquo;，他们掌握神秘的宗教知识，属于祭司长职务，通常掌管占星学、解梦、看手相、占卜、变戏法等事。摩西时代法老宫中也有这类人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，巴比伦尼布甲尼撒宫中也有</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">但</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。博士：对埃及贤人的普遍称谓</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11)
    </FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">337.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟受神默示解梦，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟受神默示解梦，表明：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">正是神在掌管法老之梦；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神有时让那些高贵、傲慢之人处于困境，使他们不得不寻求神的智慧；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神的王权俨然统治世俗的王权：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不论身份贵贱，那些与神同在、担负先知使命之人，能使世俗的君王屈服。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">338.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老听约瑟解梦后的对策是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老听约瑟解梦后的对策是，法老认为约瑟才是担任那个高官治理埃及地的人选。于是法老立即任命约瑟为埃及的宰相。约瑟确实在法老面前使神得荣耀</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">32)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，而且神也在法老面前奖赏约瑟，赐他丰富的荣誉。约瑟一生体现了&ldquo;先苦难后得荣耀&rdquo;，充分预表主在十字架上受苦、复活、升天，最终拥有天地所有的权柄</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">腓</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5-11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。在此意义上，约瑟是旧约时代最好的基督模型。
         </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">339.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老如何对待约瑟？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老使约瑟在埃及国内成为掌管所有事务的笫二把手，使他治理埃及全地。法老摘下手上打印的戒指，戴在约瑟的手上，给他穿上细麻衣，把金链戴在他的颈项上。又叫约瑟坐他的副车，喝道的在前呼叫说：&ldquo;跪下！&rdquo;这样，法老派他治理埃及全地。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">340.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老任命约瑟为宰相的特点是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">法老发布任命约瑟为宰相的手谕</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">41)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，经过相关手续</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">43)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。约瑟正式上任，法老又附加了两项：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为约瑟命名埃及新名；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">把国家贵族阶层祭司长的女儿许配给约瑟。法老这些作法，是为了巩固约瑟在埃及社会的身份及地位，以防有人对他持有偏见或藐视。
         </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">341.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">把粮食积存&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">把粮食积存&rdquo;：
不只是为了法老和埃及。神始终关心迦南地的雅各家族，在约瑟背后主管一切，要把选民引领到埃及，直到迦南地的罪恶满盈</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(15</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。神通过约瑟预备一切。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">342.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟给两子玛拿西和以法莲起名的意义何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟给两子玛拿西</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">就是&ldquo;神使之忘了&rdquo;的意思</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，因为他说：&ldquo;神使我忘了一切的困苦和我父的全家。&rdquo;他给次子起名叫以法莲</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">就是&ldquo;使昌盛&rdquo;的意思</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，因为他说：&ldquo;神使我在受苦的地方昌盛。&rdquo;
 </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">343.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">丰年和荒年何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">正如约瑟预告，灾荒临到了埃及，严重程度使大家忘了前七年的丰收</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">31)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。法老绝对信任约瑟所定的对策</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">55)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。约瑟运用神给他的智慧，出色的管理，为神所定的计划作出重大贡献。连续七年的史无前例约大饥荒，达成约瑟和他兄弟相见约契机，这是此次大饥荒背后隐藏的意义。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">42</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">344.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">全地大饥荒，神看顾雅各一家的意义何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当全地大饥荒约时候，神的关心始终在迦南地希伯仑的雅各一家。充分体现：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">圣经记载纯粹以选民为中心的历史</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">43</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">选民的历史彻底在神的主权护理之下；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">即使面对污秽罪恶的人类，神最终要把他们引向自己美善的旨意之中</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">145</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；罗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">345.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各差派十个儿子去埃及买粮食有何重要意义？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">除小儿子便雅悯外，雅各差派十个儿子去埃及买粮食，因为他考虑旷野路途的危险，另外埃及的粮食可能接人口定量出售，想一次多买些粮食。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">346.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">成全</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">20</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年前约瑟在迦南地作的第一个梦的意义和教训是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">成全</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年前约瑟在迦南地作的第一个梦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的意义和教训：约瑟的众兄长认为，卖掉约瑟就可以破碎他的梦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，神却偏偏利用这件事成就约瑟的梦。日后，当约瑟回忆自己一生时，明白这一事实，谦卑地告白这一切全是出于神</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(45</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5-8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。本事件的教训：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">无论怎样的势力，都不能阻挡神的旨意。</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神在成就自己的旨意时，深深介入到人间发生的每一件事。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">347.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">下在监里</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">天&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">下在监里</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">天&rdquo;：对约瑟的哥哥们来说，这可能是反省的机会。他们虽无罪，如今他们却被因禁，应该能够回想起曾被他们无辜扔进坑里的约瑟</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，这三天成了真心悔改的机会。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">348.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">血和罪向我们追讨&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">根据挪亚的思想</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(9</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">6)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，神曾对他说：&ldquo;凡流人血的，他的血也必被人所流&rdquo;。这种思想日后在摩西的律法中被定为赎回产业者的规矩</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">民</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">35</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">19</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">19</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">12)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">349.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为何把西缅捆绑？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">西缅是杀害闪族人的主谋</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">49</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，在谋害约瑟时他可能也最积极；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">当年流便反对谋害约瑟</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，那么除了流便，西缅就是最大的。
                </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">350.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">你可以杀我的两个儿子&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">流便用自己两个儿子的性命，担保便雅悯的安全，使父亲可以相信他们。从多坍事件中也能看出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，流便作为长子，责任性和兄弟情感都超越其他兄弟。族长时代，家长制度下，父亲掌握子女的生死权。面对危险，流便悲壮的誓言，以合法的方式将自己的两个儿子的性命交在雅各手里。从所多玛城事件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、神像事件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(31</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">32)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、他玛事件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(38</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，可以看出父亲对子女的绝对权利。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">351.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">白发苍苍，悲悲惨惨地下阴间&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">白发苍苍，悲悲惨惨地下阴间&rdquo;：指&ldquo;老人悲痛的死亡&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">31)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各听到约瑟死亡的消息，他也曾撕裂衣服，痛心地说过这话</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">35)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。表达如果便雅悯受害，自己&ldquo;如死一般，痛苦悲伤&rdquo;。
阴间：希伯来人认为，人无论善恶死后居住的地方，指地下世界。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">352.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">再去，&hellip;籴些粮来&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各看到当时饥荒事态的严重性，也清楚儿子再去埃及的境况</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。但他仍然让儿子再次下埃及。&ldquo;籴些粮来&rdquo;，&ldquo;些&rdquo;不是指少量，是东方人表达一定数量的方式，意为&ldquo;买些粮&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(43</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">353.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为什么称便雅悯为童子？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">便雅悯当时虽已二十二、三岁，但与犹大相差二十岁，又是特别保护的对象。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">354.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大为便雅悯作保和情愿永远担罪，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大为便雅悯作保意为&ldquo;我负责便雅悯的安全&rdquo;。情愿永远担罪：悲壮的誓言，若发生意外，愿意在父亲面前一辈子成为罪人，甘心接受父亲的任何惩罚。以雅各家族被驱逐、剥夺合法的继承权、受咒诅。事情顺利结束，犹大的自我牺牲精神得到了补偿，雅各大大地祝福地</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(49</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">8-12)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">355.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">俯伏在地，向他下拜&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">二十二年前，约瑟的兄长们在迦南地多坍取笑约瑟，戏弄他说&ldquo;看你怎么实现你的梦&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，通过神奇妙的安排，他们在不知不觉中成就了那个梦。一个不变的真理：神所赐属灵的梦必然成就。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">356.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">那老人家平安吗？何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟敢担心过去疼爱自己的父亲，在饥荒中是否安然无恙，他从小特别孝敬父亲</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">357.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">爱弟之情发动&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">爱弟之情发动&rdquo;，被译为&ldquo;如燃烧&rdquo;，指烧得灼热导致心脏缩紧的状态，表示怜悯不能抑制为兴奋。体现约瑟见到同母兄弟便雅悯的心情。约瑟尽力抑制自己的领袖威严及丰富的感情。这种心情酷似神对选民火般的怜悯和爱意</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">103</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">13</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">49</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">15</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">54</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">8-10</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；何</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">11</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">8</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">9)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">358.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">摆三席的原因，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">摆三席的原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">埃及严格的阶级制度。约瑟作为埃及的宰相，又是祭司长级别，不能与下级埃及人一同吃饭；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">埃及排他性餐桌的礼仪。埃及人不可与被视为低贱的希伯来人一同吃饭。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">359.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">便雅悯&hellip;多</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">倍&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> &ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">便雅悯&hellip;多</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">倍&rdquo;，
意即超过定量食物。古代近东风俗不要求客人全部吃完，只是出于尊敬和爱意，表示他是特别尊贵的客人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">撒上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22-24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。埃及人认为&ldquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5&rdquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">代表&ldquo;完全&rdquo;、&ldquo;充分&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(45</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。或许约瑟也想试探兄弟们心中是否仍存留&ldquo;残忍的嫉妒心&rdquo;，象过去对待自己那样，故特别优待便雅悯。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">44</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">360.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家族大团圆的意义何在？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家族大团圆通过家族每个成员的努力而完成：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各把拉结所生的最后一个儿子送到埃及，表明他已放弃老年人固有多单纯感情和偏爱；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟没有对兄弟们进行报复，而是给他们机会；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为了保护便雅悯，犹大情愿放弃自己的性命</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">33)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，这种行为也代表包括流便</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">37)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在内的众兄弟的立场。正是由于这种忘我精神和谦让行为，曾经由于嫉妒和罪恶分离的十二个兄弟，借着宽恕和爱重新聚集到一起。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">361.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">银杯&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟为了加罪便雅悯，将其扣留在埃及，所作的刻意的安排。约瑟想到二十三年前的多坍事件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18-28)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，想通过这件事，考验兄弟们对便雅悯的态度。银杯：原指&ldquo;银子&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(silver)(23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">362.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">占卜&rdquo;何意？约瑟有&ldquo;占卜&rdquo;行为吗？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">占卜&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(divine)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，源于蛇爬行</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">时发出的&ldquo;咝咝&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(hiss)
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">声，其含义发展成&ldquo;喃喃耳语&rdquo;、&ldquo;念咒语&rdquo;。暗示占卜是撒但的行为。在埃及，将酒杯倒满水，先向邪灵祷告，然后观察水的状况进行占卜。这与神的旨意完全相斥。摩西律法禁止占卜</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">利</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9-14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。敬拜神的约瑟绝不会有这种行为，这可能约瑟只是为了伪装自己是埃及人，人都知道埃及占卜的人特别重视这个杯子。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">363.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大为便雅悯求情的话语有何意义？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大为便雅悯求情的话语的意义：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">极其谦卑</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">极有孝心</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20-31)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">绝对的自我牺牲</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">32-34)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。纵使他犯过见不得人的他玛事件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(38</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12-18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，也能得到父亲临终前弥赛亚性祝福：&ldquo;犹大啊！你弟兄们必赞美你&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(49</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">364.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">命与&hellip;命相连&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">命与&hellip;命相连&rdquo;：字面意思为&ldquo;灵魂牵系在灵魂里&rdquo;，有力说明父亲雅各和儿子便雅悯之间不可断割的纽带关系。
   </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">365.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">替这童子作我主的奴仆，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大发自热切的兄弟之情和至诚孝心的祈求，借着自我牺牲宣言达到高潮，他的态度和提议完全通过了约瑟的考验。正是犹大的这种牺牲精神，解开了雅各家中的所有问题。犹大爱与行为并行的话语，是当今信徒应该效法实践的榜样。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">45</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">366.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">和弟兄相认&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">之前，约瑟一直努力掩饰自己的身份</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">43</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，现在不再有这个必要。因为：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">哥哥们已真正悔改</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(42</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们对年迈父亲</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">130</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的孝心</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19-32)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">也得到证实；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他们对弟弟便雅悯怀着纯洁的爱</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(44</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">33</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
      </FONT></FONT>
</P>
