<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">367.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟放声大哭&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟放声大哭意思是：他再也忍不住自己压抑的感情，放声大哭。这使我们看到，约瑟虽贵为埃及宰相，却设有忘记纯洁的亲情；也表明他从严厉的宰相</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(37</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，回转成为雅各第十一个儿子。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">368.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">我是约瑟&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">我是约瑟&rdquo;
表明他此时是宽恕与和解的人，而不是报复者，因为他哥哥们已经悔改。同样被钉十字架的耶稣</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">36)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，总有一天手握天上的权柄出现在我们面前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&#20157;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；路</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，对悔改的人，&#31042;是救赎主；对没有悔改的人，&#31042;是审判的主</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">31-46)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。
       </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">369.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神&hellip;你们以先&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为了安慰众兄弟，约瑟在</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">45</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5-9</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">节六次见证发生在自己身上的一切是神主权的护理安排。可以看出约瑟对兄弟的爱。兄弟们的恐惧，由多年后仍不能摆脱其阴影</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(50</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">15)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">可以看出。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">370.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">大施拯救&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">大施拯救&rdquo;：不仅指在大饥荒中要拯救雅各一家的性命，也包括含属灵的拯救，是指借着将要来的基督实现的。
        </FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">371.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">差我到这里来的&hellip;乃是神&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">差我到这里来的&hellip;乃是神&rdquo;是强调即使兄弟们由于嫉妒犯罪，神依然能完成自己旨意的目的。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">372.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">颈项上&hellip;亲嘴&hellip;哭&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">颈项上&hellip;亲嘴&hellip;哭&rdquo;：是宽恕的泪水及和好的场面。此刻，对雅各的儿子们来说，不需要更多的言语，只要常情的拥抱和爱心的亲吻</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">37)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。泪水代表心中真实的感情。这是雅各的儿子们真正成为以色列共同体的感人场面</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">133</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，正如神与罪人和好一样</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林后</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。圣经要求兄弟间要和好</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">373.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">埃及地的美物&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">埃及地的美物&rdquo;：指歌珊地是肥沃的下埃及地区，属兰塞境内</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(47</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">6</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">11)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">374.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从埃及地带着车辆去&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从埃及地带着车辆去&rdquo;：埃及多有平原、旷野，马车非常发达</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">14</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">6</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。约瑟家族可以使用王室马车，证明他们为贵宾。埃及最高统治者如此的款待，对雅各家族决心移居埃及起了很大的作用。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">375.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各为何表明约瑟此时是宽恕与和解的人，看见约瑟打发来接他的车辆，心就苏醒了？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各的儿子们承认当年约瑟没有被野兽咬死，而是被他们卖到埃及，报告了在埃及发生的一切，埃及宫中派来的马车作为物证。这时雅各解开了所有疑团，喜乐与惊喜使他原本麻木的心变为温馨。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">46</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">377.</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以色列&hellip;到&#21029;是巴，献给他父亲以撒的神，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以色列&hellip;到&#21029;是巴，献给他父亲以撒的神，雅各的名字变成立约的新名</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(32</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18)&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以色列&rdquo;，说明他们移居埃及的意义不单是为了躲避饥荒，而是雅各作为代表人物按照神应许的行动，将要在他后裔中</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">形成以色列民族。雅各离开希伯伦</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，来到迦南边境的别是巴</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">33</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，为曾与父亲以撒立约的神筑坛，再次确认移居到试炼地</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">26</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">埃及，是否真是神的旨意。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">378.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神在异象中&hellip;雅各！雅各！&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神在异象中&hellip;雅各！雅各！&rdquo;：异象和梦是旧约时代神重要的启示途径，为了启示神的旨意</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(37</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各！雅各！神特意重复&ldquo;雅各&rdquo;这一名字，目的是使雅各回忆过去的岁月，告诉他神始终与他保持相交，借此安慰他。让他确信别是巴之约必然成就，正如伯特利之约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13-15)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">一样。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">379.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家族移居埃及，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家族移居埃及，是亚伯拉罕蒙召</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">215</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年之后，雅各</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">130</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">岁，大慨在主前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1876</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年左右。这是救赎史的核心</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">--&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出埃及事件&rdquo;的前奏，根据神的旨意，雅各离开亚伯拉罕、以撒，及自己生活过的立约之地，终于下定决心走向埃及。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">380.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为何雅各家族移居埃及的人数有所不同？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各家族移居埃及的人数：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">六十六人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(46</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">26)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，不包括雅各、埃及的约瑟、玛拿西和以法莲；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">七十人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(46</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">27</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">5)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，加上前面除去的四人；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">七十五人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">14</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；七十士译本</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，&ldquo;七十&rdquo;这个数字与移居事件相关，目的是为了体现神完全的护理。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">381.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟让雅各家人住在歌珊地，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟让雅各家人住在歌珊地，原因：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">歌珊地：适于放牧，远离埃及人居住地；既有利于维持本行，还能防止埃及人同化。最适合保持固有的民族性和纯洁的宗教性；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">位于边境地带，有利于后裔移居迦南地。这体现约瑟和雅各坚信后裔将回归迦南地的应许</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(46</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">15</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">47</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">382.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">挑出五个人&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">埃及人认为&ldquo;五&rdquo;在数字中最有意义，所以最喜欢这个数字</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(43</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">34</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">42</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">22)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，看来约瑟向法老引见他兄弟的时候，一切都精心而机智地作了准备。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">383.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">来到这地寄居&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">寄居&rdquo;
指&ldquo;暂时居住&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(12</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">10</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">20</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">35</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">37)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。这表示他们也随先祖的信仰，坚信回归迦南地的应许，这种意识成了日后出埃及事件的背景。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">384.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">歌珊地&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">歌珊地&rdquo;：
此地肥沃，而且作为埃及的边境，也是战略要塞</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(46</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">31-34)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。法老把如此重要的地方让给以色列，可以看出他对约瑟的绝对信任，以及约瑟不可忽视的影响力。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">385.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各为法老祝福，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">旧约时代，族长的祝福权根据神和亚伯拉罕之间的生死之约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(12</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。族长也肩负家庭的祭司，能以神的祭司身份为他人祝福。雅各对法老的善意充满感恩，祝福他个人的平安与繁荣。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">386.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">兰塞&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">兰塞&rdquo;：摩西时代命名</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的歌珊新名，狭义指歌珊地国库的名称。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">387.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">都各归各城&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">各城&rdquo;
指当年大丰收时储存粮食的地方</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(41</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">48)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。约瑟施行全埃及范围的大搬迁，是为了能迅速有效地供应粮食。&ldquo;各归&rdquo;一词的希伯来语词根，不象七十士译本或武加大译本那样，被理解为&ldquo;成了仆人&rdquo;，这是不正确的。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">388.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">常俸&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"> &ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">常俸&rdquo;
指从国库中&ldquo;交付的一定数量的物品&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">箴</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；结</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。在古埃及祭政一致的社会中，给予以法老为首的统治阶层祭司的特权。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">389.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">为什么说约瑟施行的制度是善政，而不是暴政？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟施行的制度是善政，而不是暴政，原因是：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">与世界各国的纳税制度相比，交纳收成的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1/5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">作为税款，决非残酷条件；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">古时，经济上无自立能力的人往往自愿成为仆人，这时的主仆关系并不是剥削者和被剥削者的关系，而是以顺从为条件的保护者和被保护者的关系。所以众百姓钦佩约瑟的政策，甘愿成为他的仆人，自由的佃农而非奴隶</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(47</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">390.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">所葬的地方&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">所葬的地方&rdquo;
指亚伯拉罕从赫人手中买下的迦南地希伯伦的&ldquo;麦比拉洞&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(23</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">19</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">20)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。雅各的嘱咐体现出他确信迦南地才是以色列的真正基业，他相信有一天后裔会占领此地，以及</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">对列祖表示自己的情意；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">期望他的后裔不要留恋埃及地的安逸，要仰望立约之地，雅各希望这些期望日后都得以成就</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(50</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">13)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">391.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在床头上敬拜神&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各已经寿高体弱，只好在床头上敬拜神</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">王上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">47</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">48)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。他寄居的生涯，在祷告和感恩中结尾。
</FONT></FONT>
</P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">48</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">392.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟带着两个儿子玛拿西和以法莲同去访问雅各，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟带着两个儿子同去，让孙子探访祖父雅各，由于他们是埃及女人所生</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(41</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">50-52)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，约瑟想通过立约的父亲认可，使儿子成为&ldquo;以色列成员&rdquo;。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">393.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">何以雅各说以法莲和玛拿西这两个儿子是我的？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各不顾约瑟两个儿子的出生环境和血统，将他们纳入救赎史的成员，等于起誓把他们当作以色列家族独立的一员公平对待，而不是让他们作约瑟支派的两个支派。日后这一应许如实成就，以法莲和玛拿西和约瑟的其他兄弟一样，被视作雅各的亲生儿子，各自作为一个支派参与分配迦南地</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">民</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1-16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">34</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">394.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各特别强调拉结的死亡，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各特别强调拉结的死亡，是想说明他分给约瑟两份基业的理由，表明他深爱着拉结和迦南地。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">395.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">神又使我得见你的儿子，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">经过所有的试炼，雅各认识到神深奥的主权性护理和丰盛的恩典，以诚实感谢和喜乐的心发出感慨。信徒时刻不要忘记：神的试炼越大，将来恩典和祝福也越大</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">94</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">396.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">右手或右边，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在古代社会，尤其对希伯来人来说，右手或右边具有特别的意义。右手象征能力和权能</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">15</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">6-12</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；申</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">33</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；徒</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">3</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">7)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，右边是蒙辐的人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">出</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">29</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">20</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">25</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">33</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">1</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">16</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">17)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">和贵人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">王上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">2</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">19)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">所占的位子。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">397.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">按在&hellip;头上&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">按手平放在头上，圣经第一次出现按手祝福的形式。此后按手仪式为托付责任或将属灵恩赐传给他人的形式。新、旧约普遍使用。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">398.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">救赎我脱离一切患难的那使者&rdquo;何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">救赎我脱离一切患难的那使者&rdquo;指&ldquo;从一切罪恶中，救赎我的那使者&rdquo;，雅各第一次告白耶和华是自己的救赎者，即赎回产业者。雅各的一生是苦难的一生，当他回忆起自己遭遇的苦难、那位从以扫手中拯救自己的雅博渡口的使者</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(32</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24-29)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，由衷发出这样的信仰告白。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">399.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各给以法莲更大的祝福，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟希望玛拿西继承长子的祝福，但雅各却从灵里清楚看见神已定好的安排，所以给次子以法莲赐予更大的祝福。只有依靠神绝对的主权性护理，才能够理解</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">罗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10-23)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，次子优先或选择次子的原理</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">即亚伯代替该隐、以撒代替以实玛利、雅各代替以扫等</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">400.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">他</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">玛拿西</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的兄弟</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以法莲</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">将来比他还大&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以法莲支派将远远胜过玛拿西支派。经士师时代到王国分裂时代，从数量及指挥能力方面，以法莲支派超越玛拿西支派的预言如实成就</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；赛</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">401.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">使你如以法莲、玛拿西一样，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">使你如以法莲、玛拿西一样：意思是预言日后以色列百姓会以以法莲和玛拿西的繁荣作为祝福词。正如预言所示，今天在希伯来社会，这句话成为表示&ldquo;祝福&rdquo;的格言。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">402.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">我&hellip;用弓用刀&hellip;夺的&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各提到将要实现的</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">450</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">年后</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">征服迦南壮举，好似在自己手中已完成，但不是用过去时态，而是用将来进行时。&ldquo;我&rdquo;是雅各将后裔与自己同等看待。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">49</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">403.
</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各临终的预言性遗言有何特征？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各蒙圣灵感动，通过遗言，生动地预示以弥赛亚降临为核心的以色列民族史。特征：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">预言证明，日后展开的选民历史是神的救赎史，包含在神的主权计划内；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">从挪亚</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">25-27)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">开始，所有对族长的预言，都是启示最发展的救赎史预言；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">按利亚</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(49</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3-15)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、两个妾</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(49</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16-21)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、拉结</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(49</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">22-27)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">的母系顺序预言；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">重大的预言，在雅各临终前肉身最虚弱时宣布，表明神启用弱者来完成奇事</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">林前</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">27-29</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；林后</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">坦诚指出每个儿子的善恶，并对此进行祝福或咒诅，从中可以感受到报应的原理。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">404.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各反复强调&ldquo;听&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各反复强调&ldquo;听&rdquo;，因为他知道临终的紧迫性和启示的重要性。雅各的预言包含着神对世界的统治，未来历史的发展，弥赛亚降临等救赎史中的重大事件。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">405.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各对十二子祝福的象征各如何？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各的十二个儿子将构成为以色列的十二个支派。旧约的以色列的十二个支派演变成新约基督的十二个门徒，最后形成神国的十二个根基</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">14)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。以色列的十二个支派和十二个门徒作为被拯救的所有信徒的预表</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。因此雅各对十二个儿子的预言，正是当今所有信徒的拯救启示。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">406.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">西缅和利未的刀剑是残忍的器具，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">西缅和利未的刀剑是残忍的器具：指示剑事件</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(34</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">25-29)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，雅各指出他们的残忍，好战，暴力。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">407.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大是个小狮子&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">犹大是个小狮子&rdquo;，生动地描写野兽勇猛残忍的形象。含有二种意思：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">狭意上，描写从旷野时期到王国时期，犹大支派将要担负勇敢的征服重任</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，特别用于描述大卫的勇猛；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">广意上&#38755;，预示弥赛亚将会从犹大子孙中诞生，会灭绝撒但的恶势力</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">408.&ldquo;</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">圭&rdquo;、&ldquo;直等细罗&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">圭&rdquo;
，象征王权或统治的杖</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">45</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，与日后出现的治理的杖</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">45</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">6</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；来</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">相对应，是文学表现手法，指犹大后裔将继承王权。&ldquo;直等细罗&rdquo;，
预言血统上的犹大王权统治结束之时，即是属灵犹大统治权的开始至完成</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，转折点是&ldquo;细罗&rdquo;的出现。&ldquo;细罗&rdquo;指</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有人认为是地名，犹大的统治直到细罗这个地区；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">有人理解为抽象名词，指&ldquo;平安的时候&rdquo;；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">最适当的解释，指神借着犹大支派来临的&ldquo;弥赛亚&rdquo;</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">民</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">24</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；代上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">28</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。犹大支派的地上王权代表基督永远的王权。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">409.&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以萨迦&hellip;低肩背重，成为服苦的仆人&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以萨迦的性格决定了该支派的特点和命运。低肩背重，成为服苦的仆人：预言以萨迦支派将成为被支配的阶层，在外邦民族的欺压下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">16</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">10)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">，面临苦役和困境</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">王上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">9</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">21</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；代下</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">410.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各对&ldquo;但&rdquo;的预言，有何特点？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">但&rdquo;必作道上的蛇，路中的虺。希伯来文&ldquo;虺&rdquo;指土黄色，身上带有黑色斑点，毒性很强，有角的蛇，它通常隐藏在沙丘底下，有待攻击马匹。一旦被咬即可致死。这是指但支派的特性，即如毒蛇般奸诈、袭击、扰害人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">17-31)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。另外</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(1)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">但支派是拜偶像发起人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">士</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">18</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；王上</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">12</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">29</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">、</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">30)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(2)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">以色列各支派，被数点的拯救人数，但支派被省略</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">启</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">7</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">5-8)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。有人根据这些，相信将来敌基督将从但支派出现。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">411.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各对&ldquo;约瑟&rdquo;的预言，有何特点？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">约瑟&hellip;&hellip;多结果子的树枝：预言约瑟家将会昌盛，正如栽在溪水旁的丰盛的果树</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">诗</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">。他的枝条探出墙外：指将来临到的灵魂和肉身丰满的祝福。&ldquo;天上所有的福&rdquo;：早晨的露水和适量的雨水、阳光等自然界的恩惠。&ldquo;地里所藏的福&rdquo;：使土地肥沃的泉、水。常年干旱的巴勒斯坦地带，丰富的水是最大的祝福。&ldquo;生产乳养的福&rdquo;：指顺产及多产带来多子多孙。希伯来文化认为多子多孙是神最大的祝福。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">412.</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各预言的特点是什么？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">雅各预言的特点：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(1)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">把儿子们一贯的行为牢记在心；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(2)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">在救赎史过程中，各自都要担当的使命</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">太</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">25</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">15)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(3)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">一切根据神的安排；</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">(4)</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">不从个人的角度，基于对后裔的角度。</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">第</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SPAN LANG="en-US">50</SPAN></FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">章</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">413.
&ldquo;</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">用香料将约瑟熏了&rdquo;，何意？</FONT></FONT></P>
<P CLASS="cjk" STYLE="margin-bottom: 0cm">&ldquo;<FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">用香料熏&rdquo;：
贵族死亡习俗，医学发达的古埃及人</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">耶</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">46</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">：</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">11)</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">把死尸做成木乃伊。同样，也将约瑟的遗体制成木乃伊，收殓在棺材里。过了四百年，照约瑟的遗愿葬在迦南的示剑地</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">(</FONT></FONT></SPAN></FONT><FONT FACE="新宋体, monospace"><FONT SIZE=1 STYLE="font-size: 8pt">书</FONT></FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman, serif"><SPAN LANG="en-US"><FONT FACE="新宋体,
